overlord_currency_symbol = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	#generic
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_overlord_or_above = {
				not = {
					or = {
						currency_identifiers_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dinar_algerian_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dinar_iraqi_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dinar_libyan_dinar = 1

						currency_identifiers_dinar_omanian_rial = 1

						currency_identifiers_dinar_serbian_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dinar_tunisian_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dinar_yugoslav_dinar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_australian_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_canadian_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_caribbean_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_confederate_states_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_liberian_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_new_zealand_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_sierra_leonean_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_dollar_united_states_dollar = 1
						currency_identifiers_eco_ariary = 1

# ██╔████╔██║██║   ██║██╔██╗ ██║█████╗     ██║   ███████║██████╔╝ ╚████╔╝      ███████╗ ╚████╔╝ ███████╗   ██║   █████╗  ██╔████╔██║
# ██║╚██╔╝██║██║   ██║██║╚██╗██║██╔══╝     ██║   ██╔══██║██╔══██╗  ╚██╔╝       ╚════██║  ╚██╔╝  ╚════██║   ██║   ██╔══╝  ██║╚██╔╝██║

monetary_system = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
			}
		}

		localization_key = gold_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_bimetallism_standard
		}

		localization_key = bimetallism_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_silver_standard
		}

		localization_key = silver_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_external_exchange_standard
		}

		localization_key = bimetallism_good
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_fiat_standard
				has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_system
			}
		}

		localization_key = spe_uni_good
	}
}

stokpiling_grain_status = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:grain_store_status = 1
		}
		localization_key = store_on
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:grain_release_status = 1
		}
		localization_key = release_on
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:grain_release_status = 0
			var:grain_store_status = 0
		}
		localization_key = no_order
	}
}

law_monetary_policy	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:revaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_75

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_100

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_25

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_50

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_75

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_100

	}
}
law_monetary_policy_texture	= {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
		}

		localization_key = law_no_monetary_policy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_war_economy
		}

		localization_key = law_war_economy_texture
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_revaluation_100
				var:revaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_revaluation_texture

	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_25
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_50
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_75
				has_law = law_type:law_devaluation_100
				var:devaluation_on = 1
			}
		}

		localization_key = law_devaluation_texture
	}
}

country_credit_rating_texture = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			#country_credit_rating >= 499
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}

		localization_key = AAA
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {

	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

		trigger = {

				is_reference_currency_no = yes
			}
		}

	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_strong_currency = yes
		}

	}

		trigger = {
			is_balanced_currency = yes
		}

		localization_key = balanced_currency

			is_weak_currency = yes
		}

		localization_key = weak_currency
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_extreme_weak_currency = yes
		}

		localization_key = extreme_weak_currency
	}
}

metal_barometre = {
	type = country
	log_loc_errors = no

	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate <= 0.20
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.17
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_1
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.17
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.14
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_2
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.14
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.11
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_3
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.11
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.08
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_4
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.08
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.05
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_5
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.05
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.03
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_6
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			silver_to_gold_rate < 0.03
			silver_to_gold_rate >= 0.00
		}

		localization_key = metal_barometre_7
	} 
}
